             <span class="def-num">1</span>

            <!--1a. entry title --> 
            <h2 class="vg-header"><span class="ref-src"></span> Definition of <span class="vg-sm">package</span></h2> 
            <!--3. Entry level sls --> 
            <!--4. Entry level def --> 
            <div class="vg"> 
             <!--Entry level ins (if def is present)--> 
             <div class="sb has-sn"> 
              <span class="sb-0"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn"><span class="num">1</span></span> 
                <span class="sl">archaic</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>the act or process of <a href="/dictionary/packing" class="mw_t_a_link">packing</a> </span>
               </div> </span> 
             </div> 
             <div class="sb has-sn"> 
              <span class="sb-0"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn"><span class="num">2</span> a</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a small or moderate-sized pack <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong><a href="/dictionary/parcel" class="mw_t_sx">parcel</a> </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-1"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">b</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a commodity or a unit of a product uniformly wrapped or sealed </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-2"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">c</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a preassembled unit </span>
               </div> </span> 
             </div> 
             <div class="sb has-sn"> 
              <span class="sb-0"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn"><span class="num">3</span></span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a covering wrapper or container </span>
               </div> </span> 
             </div> 
             <div class="sb has-sn"> 
              <span class="sb-0"> <span class="bs"> 
                <div class="sense"> 
                 <span class="sn"><span class="num">4</span></span> 
                 <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>something that suggests a package: such as </span>
                </div> </span> </span> 
              <span class="sb-1"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">a</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong><a href="/dictionary/package deal" class="mw_t_sx">package deal</a> </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-2"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">b</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a radio or television series offered for sale at a lump sum </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-3"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">c</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>contract benefits gained through collective bargaining </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-4"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">d</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a ready-made computer program or collection of related software </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-5"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">e</span> 
                <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a travel arrangement contract that offers for a fixed price transportation, accommodations, and often sightseeing and entertainment </span>
               </div> </span> 
              <span class="sb-6"> 
               <div class="sense"> 
                <span class="sn">f</span> 
                <span class="dt hasSdSense"> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>a collection of related items; <span class="sdsense"> <span class="sd">especially</span> <span class="dt "> <strong class="mw_t_bc">:</strong>one to be considered or acted on together 
                   <ul class="vis">
                    <li><span class="t">presented his tax <span class="mw_t_wi">package</span> to the nation</span></li>
                   </ul> </span> </span> </span>
               </div> </span> 
             </div> 
            </div>

           <div class="inner-box-wrapper"> 
            <h2 class="card-box-title">First Known Use of <i>package</i></h2> 
            <div class="card-primary-content">

       <p class="mell-gr235"><a href="/video/irregardless" ">It is in fact a real word (but that doesn't mean you should use it).</a></p> 
      </div>

       <h5><a href="/video/weird-plurals" ">Weird Plurals</a></h5>

  <script>
      require(['common', 'audioplayer', 'wodSubscribe', 'gaTracker', 'fbSdk', 'adProcessor', 'raf'], function(common, audioplayer, wodSubscribe, gaTracker, fbSdk, adProcessor) {

        //Prep page counter cookie (expiration = 10 minutes)
        var pvc = $.cookie('pvc');
        pvc = (pvc === undefined) ? 1 : (parseInt(pvc) + 1);
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (10 * 60 * 1000));
        $.cookie('pvc', pvc, { expires: date, path: '/' });

        //JC: needs to be refactored
        common.init();

        //JC: Initiating ad libraries (google slot lib, ) & initializing slots
        adProcessor.prepareAdLibraries();

        //JC: by default we use a black-list, white-list is only being used if provided (rare cases)
        if (window.mwdata.adsWhitelist  !== null) {
          adProcessor.prepareOnlyTheseAdSlots(window.mwdata.adsWhitelist);
        } else {
          adProcessor.prepareAllAdSlotsExcept(window.mwdata.adsBlacklist);
        }

        //JC: this enables audio playback everywhere (wod & definitions)
        audioplayer.init();

         //JC: Enabling WOD subscribe forms if present
        wodSubscribe.init();

        //JC: Loading google analitics libary and starting tracking
        gaTracker.init();

        //JC: special handling for spelling suggestionsand not found pages.
        if (window.mwdata.gaSpecialTracking) {
            // Track the virtual page click.
            var url = '/dictionary/' + window.mwdata.gaSpecialTracking + '/' + window.mwdata.gaSpecialTrackingWord;
            var gaCmd = function(){ga('send', 'pageview', url);};
            gaTracker.execCmd(gaCmd);
            console.log('Special tracking, type:', window.mwdata.gaSpecialTracking, url);
        }

        //JC: Facebook SDK is needed on all pages except for Home
        if (window.mwdata.isHome === false) {
          fbSdk.init();
        }
      });
    </script>
